The construction of the sentence in German mirrors the original English sentence by using the same word order and structures. Here, "that solid" is translated as "dass feststehende", where "dass" is a relative pronoun and "feststehende" is the noun phrase that refers back to "One thing". The German sentence also uses the passive voice, as does the original English sentence, to emphasize the action of "becoming apparent" happening to the subject.
